<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:plural.html>plural</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>ones</a></b>)
